The Problem of Prohibiting Tobacco Seedlings in Fujian Province 88

The Anti-Smoking Association Decides to Implement its Stance

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Anti-Smoking Committee believes that the counties of Putian, Xianyou, Si'an, Nan'an, Jinjiang, Anxi, Haiyan, Zhangpu, Longxi, Nanjing, Pinghe, Yunxiao, Zhao'an, etc. in southern Fujian are preparing to plant tobacco seedlings. Military and police personnel in Fuzhou and Xiamen are allegedly colluding with organizations to protect the private transportation of opium smokers. The prohibition order has been swept away and the legal system cannot be stopped, which is deeply regrettable. Therefore, the committee members jointly submitted their resignations to the provincial government in order to clarify their responsibilities. The provincial government issued an order to comfort and retain them, and at the same time, issued a proclamation reiterating the prohibition of smoking and distributing it to various counties for posting so that the public would be fully informed. The wording of the proclamation was quite severe, stating that the prohibition of opium cultivation has been repeatedly emphasized. Recently, it has been heard that the ignorant people in various counties are still planting [tobacco]. It must be known that the government has long had the determination to prohibit smoking. If anyone violates the prohibition order, they will be severely punished according to law. Cultivating tobacco was originally intended to make a profit, but the result is that both the principal and the interest are lost, and they also fall into the legal net, to be severely punished. There is no benefit in doing so, so why not reform early? If anyone dares to resist eradication by the crowd, they will be punished by dispatching troops along the way. At that time, regardless of the innocent or the guilty, it is bound to harm the neighbors. Regardless of military police officials, wealthy gentry, or bad gentry, if collusion is detected, they will be immediately severely punished. It is now heard that the Anti-Smoking Committee has scheduled a general meeting in the coming days to formulate measures to eradicate tobacco seedlings and prohibit the private transportation of opium smokers, which will be submitted to the provincial government for implementation. If it is still ineffective, the committee will dissolve itself to apologize to the people of the country. (October 29th)

Hubei Emergency Relief Association 89

Reorganized into a Post-Flood Relief Committee

American Wheat Will Be Shipped to Hubei in Six Installments for Distribution

The Issue of Rent Reduction and Exemption Has Been Completely Resolved

Hankou Correspondence: The Hubei Flood Emergency Relief Committee is now ending its emergency relief efforts as the floodwaters have gradually receded and the disaster victims have returned to their hometowns. All post-disaster matters must also be planned for early. Therefore, a meeting of all committee members was convened on October 30th to discuss the matter. It was decided to reorganize the committee into the Hubei Post-Flood Relief Committee. The internal organization was divided into nine sections, including general affairs, investigation, review, fundraising, relief affairs, public works, storage, accounting, and procurement. The five committee members Zhu Huaibing, Ma Dengying, He Hengfu, Chen Jingyu, and Cai Fuqing were appointed to draft the organizational outline and submit it to the next meeting for discussion before implementing the reorganization and establishment. The income of the Emergency Relief Committee from July 29th to October 30th was more than 654,000 yuan, including 170,000 yuan from the central government. The expenditure was more than 536,000 yuan, with an actual balance of more than 110,000 yuan, which will be announced according to the accounts. It is heard that after the reorganization of the committee, the emergency relief will be stopped. The problem of food shortages in various counties will be resolved by the Wuhan Office of the Disaster Area Working Group of the National Government Relief General Association with American wheat relief. The quantity of American wheat and the delivery deadline have been allocated and stipulated by the General Association. The office has received a telegram from Zhu Qinglan, urging it to prepare immediately. The telegram stated that the purchase of American wheat has already started and the first and second ships can arrive in Shanghai in the coming days. Regarding emergency relief, it should be allocated in advance for planning and distribution. Hubei Province has been assigned 15,000 tons, which will be delivered in six installments in October, November, December, January, February, and March. Please organize and implement it quickly according to the regulations of the inspection and distribution guidelines. Distribution tickets should be distributed according to the amount, so that there is no shortage of food or the situation of storing wheat without distribution. If there is a need to borrow relief grain from local grain merchants for emergency relief, the amount can be deducted when deciding on the amount of inspection and distribution. Emergency relief should start at the same time as the work relief, limited to households with no able-bodied men. Those who can work should be recruited into the work ranks and receive relief according to their work to maintain themselves and their families. As for the regulations on unloading wheat, the total amount of American wheat in the Wuhan area is 15,000 tons, which will be unloaded in Wuxue, Hankou, Xindi, Huangshigang, and Jianli. 300 tons each in October, 600 tons each in November, 750 tons each in December, 600 tons each in January, 600 tons each in February, and 150 tons each in March, totaling 3,000 tons for each place. As for the Wuhan side, food has gradually become available for assistance. All refugee shelters except the first one have been closed, and all porridge factories have also been stopped. After the American wheat arrives, work relief will be implemented to avoid the displacement of disaster victims. In addition, the rent issue has been resolved after several consultations among various parties. (1) Those whose houses were not flooded during the flood period will pay rent as usual (houses that were not flooded are no more than 20-30). (2) Those whose houses were flooded downstairs but can live upstairs will be exempted from half of the original rent from the date of the flood to the date of the flood receding, but those whose rent is less than 100 yuan per room will be exempted from 2/3, and those whose rent is more than 100 yuan should pay 1/2 of the rent. If the upstairs and downstairs tenants are separate, the upstairs tenant will bear it. (3) Houses along Jisheng Road will be exempted from rent from the date of the flood to the date of the flood receding. (4) Rent arrears before the flood and rent due after the flood will be paid in full. (5) All landlords and tenants who have resolved their rent issues before this method is determined are not included in this limit. The above decisions will be submitted to the provincial government by the municipal government for record and public notice. (October 30th)

Anhui People 90

Appeal for the Combined Construction of the North and South Huai River Dikes

Bengbu Correspondence: Among the counties hit hardest by this year's floods in Anhui Province, those along the Huai River were the most severely affected. In order to provide both disaster relief and fundamental solutions, the National Government Flood Relief Committee purchased a large amount of American wheat to carry out work relief and build the Huai River dikes. The committee requested the Huai River Guidance Committee to dispatch surveying teams to conduct on-site surveys and schedule the construction. The first and second teams of the surveying team have already gone to the middle and upper reaches to carry out segment-by-segment surveys. However, the Huai River Middle and Upper Reaches Flood Control Dike Plan formulated by the Huai River Guidance Committee stipulates that the dike route will only be built on the left bank (i.e., the north bank) from Honghekou in Huoqiu to Fushan in Wuhe. The Anhui North Flood Relief Committee has expressed dissatisfaction upon hearing this, believing that the Huai River dikes must be built simultaneously on both the north and south banks. If only the north dike is built, the south bank will inevitably become a ditch. The committee held a meeting of the Executive Committee last night (the 31st) to discuss this matter and decided to telegraph the National Government Flood Relief Committee to build both the north and south dikes of the Huai River, stating that "It has recently been heard that the Huai River Guidance Committee's surveyors have come to Bengbu one after another to carry out segment-by-segment surveys and build the north dike of the Huai River, and the south bank will not be constructed for the time being. The people on both sides of the Huai River are shocked and suspicious upon hearing this. It is secretly investigated that the Huai River dikes on both sides were destroyed at the same time during this year's floods. If the north dike is built, the south bank will inevitably become a ditch, which will inevitably lead to disputes. The [Flood Relief Committee] intends to treat both sides equally. We earnestly request that both sides be considered and built simultaneously, so that work relief can be universal and future troubles can be avoided. (Flood Relief Committee of Anhui North Kowtow to the East) (November 1st)

Legislative Yuan Passes 91

Regulations on the Administration of Narcotic Drugs

The revised Regulations on the Administration of Narcotic Drugs were revised and passed by the Legislative Yuan at its 169th meeting on the 31st of last month. The regulations are recorded as follows: (Article 1) The import and sale of narcotic drugs shall be administered in accordance with these Regulations. (Article 2) Narcotic drugs in these Regulations refer to opium, morphine, cocaine, heroin, and similar toxic substances or compounds used for medical and scientific purposes. (Article 3) The import and

Page 8

The distribution of narcotic drugs shall be the responsibility of the general manager designated by the Ministry of Interior. The amount of narcotic drugs imported shall be determined annually by the State Council. The manufacture of narcotic drugs shall be prohibited until regulations for special manufacturing permits are enacted. (Article 4) If provinces or municipalities under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan need narcotic drugs, the provincial government or the municipal government shall designate pharmacies to manage the distribution. (Article 5) When the general manager's office imports narcotic drugs from abroad, the Ministry of Interior shall issue a certificate. The certificate shall state the type, quantity, purpose, and purchase process. (Article 6) The port of entry for narcotic drugs shall be limited to Shanghai. (Article 7) When the distribution agency purchases and transports narcotic drugs from the general manager's office, the provincial government or the municipal government under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan shall issue a certificate each time. The items stated in the certificate shall be in accordance with the provisions of the second paragraph of Article 5. The certificate shall be sent by the certificate holder to the Ministry of Interior for sealing. (Article 8) The import quantity and distribution of narcotic drugs shall be announced by the Ministry of Interior at least once a year. (Article 9) Local hospitals, doctors, dentists, veterinarians, pharmacists, or medical schools that need narcotic drugs shall submit a written statement of reasons, sign and seal it, and purchase them from the distribution agency. However, the weight of each purchase by hospital pharmacists or medical schools shall not exceed 50 grams, and the weight of each purchase by doctors, dentists, or veterinarians shall not exceed 10 grams. (Article 10) When the general manager's office transports narcotic drugs, it shall package them separately according to the quantity limited in the preceding article, and make a packaged envelope and seal, stating the name, weight, and price of the product, and affix them tightly. The distribution agency shall not open or change the packaging except when dispensing. (Article 11) The distribution agency shall sell narcotic drugs at the price set on the package or seal, and shall not arbitrarily increase the price. The price shall be proposed by the general manager's office and submitted to the Ministry of Interior for approval. (Article 12) The Ministry of Interior and the Opium Suppression Committee may dispatch personnel at any time to inspect the transportation and sales of the general manager's office and the distribution agencies, as well as the amount of existing products. The provincial, municipal, and county governments may dispatch personnel at any time to inspect the transportation and use of the affiliated distribution agencies, hospitals, doctors, dentists, veterinarians, pharmacists, medical schools, etc., and report the situation to the higher authorities for transfer to the Ministry of Interior and the Opium Suppression Committee. (Article 13) If the general manager's office, distribution agency, hospitals, doctors, dentists, veterinarians, pharmacists, or medical schools have any illegal or fraudulent activities, they shall be punished according to law. If the distribution agency has illegal or fraudulent activities, the pharmacy shall be ordered to close. (Article 14) The certificates issued by the Ministry of Interior shall be in quadruplicate. One copy shall be kept as a stub, one copy shall be sent to the Chinese Consulate at the place of purchase, and two copies shall be issued to the purchaser for collection. In addition to the copy retained by the customs upon import, the other copy shall be returned to the Ministry of Interior for verification after being transported to the general manager's office. (Article 15) The certificates issued by the provincial government or the municipal government under the direct jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan shall be in quadruplicate. One copy shall be kept as a stub, one copy shall be sent to the Ministry of Interior, and two copies shall be issued to the purchaser for collection. In addition to the copy retained by the general manager's office when purchasing the drugs, the other copy shall be returned to the government that originally issued the certificate for verification after being transported to the distribution agency. Article 16)

At the end of each month, the general manager's office shall list the purchase, sale, and existing quantity of narcotic drugs and report it to the Ministry of Interior. At the end of each month, each distribution agency shall list the purchase, sale, and existing quantity of narcotic drugs and report it to the local government for review and transfer to the Ministry of Interior. At the end of each month, each hospital, doctor, dentist, veterinarian, pharmacist, medical school, etc. that purchases narcotic drugs shall list the purchase, sale, use, and existing quantity of narcotic drugs and report it to the local government for review and transfer to the Ministry of Interior. (Article 17) The Ministry of Interior shall, based on the statistical reports submitted by the general manager's office and the distribution agencies, list them periodically and submit them to the Executive Yuan for presentation to the National Government for verification, and shall also send them to the Opium Suppression Committee. (Article 18) The format of certificates, packages, seals, and statistical reports shall be determined by the Ministry of Interior. (Article 19) All certificates for purchasing and transporting narcotic drugs issued by any agency before the implementation of these Regulations shall be invalid. (Article 20) Public offices in charge of testing and manufacturing drugs shall, when narcotic drugs are needed for their duties, list the names and quantities of the drugs and, after being approved by the Ministry of Interior, transport them to the General Manager's Office for purchase. (Article 21) The methods for suppressing divinyl ether drugs for medical and scientific purposes shall be governed by the provisions of these Regulations. (Article 22) These Regulations shall be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Siam Increases Tax on Chinese Immigrants 93

Each Person Must First Pay a Tax of Forty Baht

To Be Implemented Starting November 16

After the Siamese government promulgated new immigration regulations, the most affected areas are Chaozhou, Shantou, and Haikou. More than 10,000 people travel from these two ports to Siam every month. Last week, Taikoo Yanghang received news from Singapore that the British Straits Settlements government will ban Chinese laborers from entering the country starting from New Year's Day next year. Ships at the four ports of Shantou, Xiamen, Hong Kong, and Haikou are only allowed to carry first-class cabin passengers and cargo. Third-class tickets are not allowed to be sold. Today, Fulin Yanghang also received a telegram from Bangkok, Siam, that the Siamese government will increase the tax on Chinese immigrants starting from November 16. Each person must pay a head tax of forty baht when they land. In this situation, the South Seas Islands are no longer accessible to our compatriots. (October 24)

Local Communications

Chongming 95

Disputes After the Separation of Chongming and Qidong Counties. Qidong County, on the north bank of the Yangtze River estuary, was originally the outer sand territory under the jurisdiction of Chongming County. It is separated by a river surface of forty li. Previously, due to the inconvenience of administrative facilities, the provincial government decided in the 17th year of the Republic of China to change the outer sand into the Qidong County seat and submitted it to the National Government for record. Recently, the gentry of Chongming requested a re-merger due to the countless difficulties since the separation. The provincial government handed it over to the three departments of civil affairs, finance, and construction for joint review. After the provincial government's decision on the 30th of last month was finalized, it was not convenient to change it. The difficulties between the two counties will be resolved by the three departments of civil affairs, finance, and construction, convening the two county magistrates to properly resolve them. It is heard that the province has scheduled to convene a meeting of the two county magistrates in Shanghai in the middle of this month. The heads of various bureaus, representatives of various agencies, and representatives from all walks of life will also attend the discussion.

Suzhou 96

Cai Tingkai's troops will open to Suzhou, and Chen Mingshu's troops are ordered to garrison the Beijing-Shanghai Railway. The division headquarters of the Sixtieth Division of Cai Tingkai's troops has decided to be stationed in Suzhou. Yesterday, Vice Officer Meng was sent to Suzhou to discuss all matters with the county government. The troops are expected to arrive in Suzhou within a week.

Feiyun Ferry Kidnapped and Ransom Released Fourteen People. The Tongyuan Bureau's Feiyun ferry, which runs between Dongshan and Suzhou, departed from Shan at 8:30 AM one day and was hijacked by more than 20 lake bandits at the Tingzigang area outside the Hengjing ferry crossing at around 9:00 AM. Before leaving, they kidnapped 17 male and female passengers, as reported yesterday. Yesterday (2nd), it was learned that after detailed investigation, there were a total of 23 passengers kidnapped on the ferry. That night, the bandits interrogated the identities of the hostages one by one and released 14 poor people. Xu Huaihong, a male teacher at Fuyu Elementary School, was also among them. When releasing these 14 people, the bandits ordered them to notify the family of Chu, a wealthy household in Dongshan who was kidnapped but not released, to pay a ransom of 500,000, and the family of Xu to pay 300,000. Those remaining in the bandit den include Ms. Chuan Zhongde, the principal of the county-run Zhongxiu Girls' School, teacher Ms. Qian, and Chu, Xu, and other nine people. The bandit ship has fled to the Beiku area near Wujiang. The land police team has rushed to assist in the suppression and rescue of the hostages from danger.

It is now learned yesterday (2nd) that Chen, the county magistrate of this county, received instructions from the High Court stating that although the guards had no faults such as bribery and connivance, they did provide the prisoners with an opportunity to escape, which was extremely negligent. Jiangyin 98

The Provincial Department Rejected the Clearance of Debt Coupons. The provincial government instructed that, according to the financial department's review of Jiangyin County's request to issue local debt coupons for clearing debts, it is far from the principles of finance. All counties have been rejected uniformly. It should be ordered to continue to follow the previous instructions to find other appropriate methods and not insist on the previous proposal. After the county government received the order, it convened a meeting on the 30th to discuss and decided that since the debt coupons were not approved for issuance and the local accumulated debts could not be left unaddressed, it should submit a proposal to the provincial department to allow the collection of two cents of the original debt coupon fund's surtax to be used exclusively for repaying old debts. The Headquarters Cracked Down on Robbers on the Xicheng Road. On November 2nd, Qian Shusheng, an employee of the cocoon industry association, collected 594 yuan in cocoon tax in Wuxi and took a long-distance bus to Qingyang. He changed to a rickshaw and was robbed while passing over the Fengjing Bridge. He immediately reported it to the county government for investigation. The Su-Chang Pacification Command received a tip from an informant that the main bandit, Huang Sibao, was hiding in the Yao Ancestral Hall in Sihe. Commander Zhu immediately sent Vice Officer Han Mingfeng and others to arrest him at the Li family in Qingyang on the 30th and escorted him to the command for interrogation before handing him over to the county government for interrogation.

Changzhou 99

The Departments of Finance and Construction Urged the Payment of Construction Funds. As of recently, the Wuyi construction fund had a total deposit of more than 168,000 yuan. The province ordered that half of it, 84,000 yuan, be used to purchase public bonds for water management. Various local agencies and gentry believed that the construction fund could not be withdrawn according to the regulations promulgated by the province, and the local demand for various funds was very large. They telegraphed the provincial departments to exempt them from withdrawing the funds. On the 1st of this month, County Magistrate Zhang received a joint order from the two provincial departments of finance and construction stating that the county should calculate the number of bonds to be purchased according to half of the construction funds remaining at the end of the 19th year, temporarily deducting the 75,000 yuan deposited in the passbook, and report the withdrawal of funds for submission within the specified date.

Nantong 100

The Yijin Maru Accident Case Was Rejected for the Second Time. The Japanese merchant ship Yijin Maru collided with and sank Xu Huiyuan's cargo ship in Rengang. Xu appealed to all sectors, and the Nantong County Government submitted a report to the province and consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with the Japanese ambassador. However, the Japanese side replied with evasive words and tried to shirk responsibility. After the Ministry of Foreign Affairs investigated and verified, it rejected the reply. County Magistrate Zhang, after collecting all the evidence of the case on the same day, submitted a report to the province. One day, he received an order to forward it to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for another rejection of the points raised by the Japanese ambassador.

Rugao 101

The Recent Situation of the Dongxing Flood. The Rugao Committee for Receiving Flood Victims Along the Canal previously sent Hong, a member of the Red Swastika Society, to Dongtai and Xinghua to investigate the flood situation. According to the report from Rugao, the flood in Dongtai has slightly receded and is still passable by land. The city base of Xinghua is still sitting in the water, and only a few land routes can be passed in the city. The suburbs are still a vast expanse of water one zhang away from the city. From Haian to Dongtai, passing through Fuan, Andong, Liangduo, and other places, the water is still higher than the fields. The low-lying fields along the way in Jiangyan and Qintong are all submerged in water, with some five or six feet high and others one or two feet high. The foundations of the residents' houses have not yet left the water. The disaster situation is very serious. In the blink of an eye, the weather is severely cold, and many flood victims are still homeless, which is worrying.

Yangzhou 102

All Schools in the Urban Area Are Suspended. The schools and community education colleagues in the urban area of Jiangdu have been in arrears with seven months of teaching fees as of the end of October. They have repeatedly consulted with the newly appointed Director Jia without any solution. They held an emergency meeting at the public sports field and decided to suspend work uniformly from November 2nd and nominated members to draft a petition to resign from the education bureau and send letters to the parents of the children in each school stating their difficulties.

Please the County to Investigate and Ban the Resumption of Slaughterhouses. In order to maintain spring plowing next year, the Department of Agriculture ordered the county to close the slaughterhouses to prevent farmers from selling and slaughtering plowing cattle due to disasters. The Cattle Protection Association stated that fresh beef was sold on the market again, and there were several large and small slaughterhouses resuming operations outside Dongguan. They specifically proposed a motion at the fifth standing committee meeting to request the county to investigate and ban them, which was passed by the public. It is heard that the county has been asked to investigate and ban them in order to protect spring plowing.

Gaoyou 103

A Burning and Robbing Case Occurred in Xujiazhuang. More than 20 bandits suddenly came to Xujiazhuang in the ninth district of the county the night before last. Each of them held guns and went to the homes of farmers Xu Fulai, Xu Changyou, Xu Jiuyu, Chen Wensong, and others to search and rob. Before leaving, they burned down the residences of the four families of Xu and others. It is heard that the loss is about more than 10,000 yuan.

Qingjiang 104

The Public Security Bureau Chief is Under the Custody of the County. Zhu Ying, the chief of the Public Security Bureau of Huaiyin, previously sent his supervisor, Yuan Xuepu, to serve at the joint military and police inspection office in this county. Yuan learned that Guo Ruisheng, the company commander of the second battalion of the garrison, had purchased a box gun and 100 bullets from Guo for 130 yuan. This matter was known to Commander Liang, who ordered Regiment Commander Zeng Jirui to arrest Yuan, saying that according to the report of Company Commander Guo, he was suspected of inducing the purchase of military equipment and should be dealt with according to law. Yuan confessed that the gun was purchased by Director Zhu Ying, the money was paid by Zhu himself in the amount of thirty yuan, and he ordered someone to take one hundred yuan from the accounting office in the bureau. Commander Zeng then sent someone to seize the gun in the Public Security Bureau. Commander Liang sent a telegram to Zhang, the supervising officer of Yangzhou, and Chairman Ye of the provincial government to report the incident and sent a letter to Huaiyin County to put Zhu under custody. On the 20th of this month, Dai Boqiu, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, bailed Zhu out. On the 27th, Liang received a telegram from the supervising officer's office advocating strict punishment. Liang ordered Zhu to appear for questioning, but Zhu did not appear. He then sent another letter to County Magistrate He to put Zhu under custody to prevent him from escaping. The duties of the bureau chief are temporarily performed by Chief Supervisor Zhang Quan. Continued Report on the Closure of the Three Industries. The three industries of cloth, general merchandise, and groceries in Huaiyin all stopped business because yesterday was the deadline for sealing Japanese goods. Today, County Magistrate He invited Ye Zijun and Gu Xunru, the standing committee members of the Chamber of Commerce, to discuss solutions, but there were no results. Liu Dingxin, the chairman of the committee and the standing committee member of the Anti-Japanese Association, went to Yangzhou due to other matters, resulting in a stalemate. Today (29th), 78 shops in the city and suburbs, including 14 cloth shops, 44 general merchandise shops, and 20 grocery stores, are still closed and not doing business. In order to maintain public order, County Magistrate He invited the letter writers to talk again today, hoping to open the towels as soon as possible, but no one went. It is also heard that the large and small money shops inside and outside the city are unable to receive loans due to the closure of the three industries, and they are afraid that there will be a continued strike tomorrow. However, the members of the Anti-Japanese Association did not express much about this, only saying that they would wait for the industries to open before proceeding with the sealing procedures. As for the value of the Japanese goods occupied by the three industries, according to the registration of each industry, the silk and cloth are worth about 89,000 yuan, the general merchandise is worth about 6,800 yuan, and the groceries are worth about 6,467 yuan. In fact, it is more than this number, otherwise they would not have sacrificed the closure of business to fight for it.

Hangzhou 105

The Appeal in the Longjing Kidnapping and Murder Case Was Announced. Last year, Li Yun, a Cantonese merchant, was kidnapped by bandits at Longjing Temple in West Lake and brutally murdered in Songhe Villa. The Hangzhou District Court sentenced the bandits Wang Yang, Wang Zhuo, and Wu Jingyuan to be shot. Wang Fengshan and Wang Zhangshui were sentenced to eight months in prison for fraud. Ying Wen was acquitted. The prosecutor appealed, and the High Court concluded the trial. The appeal reason was insufficient, and the original judgment was upheld. Wang Fengshan and Wang Zhangshui were granted a two-year reprieve.

Incoming Letter

Letter from the Wu Kun Jiang Chang Tai Jia Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau 107

Recently, I read a local communication from Suzhou in your newspaper on the 1st, "Investigation by the Provincial Committee into the License Tax Dispute," which is inconsistent with the facts. The collection of tobacco and alcohol license taxes has always been contracted by merchants, resulting in many long-standing malpractices. Since this year, the Ministry of Finance has promulgated new regulations and changed it to a delegated responsibility. It is our duty to abide by the new regulations and carry out rectification to increase national revenue and eliminate long-standing malpractices. Unexpectedly, this has caused a backlash from merchants who have united through the guild to try to maintain the old contracting system. They have filed a complaint with the provincial bureau, which has been investigated by the Provincial Committee in Suzhou and found no dereliction of duty. Correspondingly, we are writing to your newspaper to make a correction to promote fairness. Sincerely, the Wu Kun Jiang Chang Tai Jia Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax Bureau, November 2, 20th year of the Republic of China.

Special Article

Women and Military Training by Wang Xiaoying 108

Since the violent Japanese troops have invaded the Eastern Province and ravaged our borders, trampling our famous cities and killing people for goods, the whole country is filled with anger, especially the young students who are driven by their patriotic zeal to dedicate themselves to the country, either volunteering to fight the enemy or organizing volunteer armies. Here, there is a question of whether schoolgirls should receive military training or not. Some say that women are naturally weaker and military affairs are not suitable for them. However, there have been women in both the East and the West who have joined the military and made contributions on the battlefield. Princess Pingyang, Hua Mulan, and Liang Hongyu of our country will always be praised by later generations. Joan of Arc of France bravely killed the enemy and turned the tide of the war. Catherine of Russia defeated Turkey and Poland, seizing vast territories. Austria's Maria Theresa used a large army to confront Frederick the Great. Elizabeth of England defeated the Spanish Armada at sea. Isabella of Spain drove out the Jews and Moors, completing national unification. But this is just in terms of individuals. It is said that the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom raised an army of hundreds of thousands, and there were 500,000 women. During the Xinhai Revolution, there was a women's Northern Expedition team. The women of ancient Sparta spent their lives in military camps. During the French Revolution, French women fought alongside men, competing to kill and not hesitating. During the European War, women from all countries went to the national crisis together and became glorious bloodshedders. Seeing this, women are not unable to participate in military affairs, but it depends on whether we have this determination. I have seen women participating in track and field competitions in sports meets everywhere, and there are countless famous female aviators in the world. Women can engage in strenuous exercise and flying, and it is easy to undergo military training.

Our country is facing a national crisis. The army, claiming to be two million strong, is brave in private matters but timid in public battles. The Japanese pirates are as venomous as snakes and scorpions and as cruel as owls. The national army has not resisted them, sitting idly by as the beautiful land is slaughtered. Women also have a natural duty to the nation and defend their homes. With the country in such danger, the only way is to prepare quickly, receive military training, unite with the people of the whole country to resist foreign aggression, endure hardship, and sweep away shame. The indigenous people of Taiwan were forced by the harsh policies of the Japanese to launch an anti-Japanese movement. The Japanese mobilized a large army to annihilate the indigenous people. The women of the indigenous people competed to commit suicide in order to send their fathers and brothers out the door. The Indian national movement has lasted for twenty years. Sarojini Naidu and other female heroes have run around shouting and awakening the Indian people. I mean that the women of our country should not take the passive way of the Taiwanese indigenous women to repay the country with one death, nor should they take the futile shouting of Sarojini Naidu and other female heroes. We believe that Japan and our country are incompatible and cannot coexist. Everyone must prepare to fight a bloody battle with the Japanese pirates. Women compatriots cannot be an exception.

There are more than 600 students in our school's Wuben Middle School department. Except for those who are too young, they are organized into a rescue team. The rest of the students are willing to receive military training. From an educational standpoint, I believe that military training for schoolgirls has unparalleled value in both peacetime and wartime. In peacetime, students all know to love the country and not forget to study, and study not forgetting to love the country. Today's students are indeed studying. If they are studying and not forgetting to love the country, it is not relying on slogans, but on a strong body to fight the enemy. How can students have a strong body? Training is indispensable. The best way to train is to receive military training. I believe that military training for women has at least the following values in peacetime: First, learn diligence; second, strengthen the body; third, elucidate reason; fourth, maintain order; fifth, respect obedience. Please analyze it again.

First, learn diligence. Except for the naturally diligent women in the agricultural and industrial classes, women in the metropolis indulge in idleness, luxury, and do not know the word diligence. Schoolgirls who receive military training get up early to wash, and they are diligent day and night, developing a habit that will not be disturbed by the outside world. Second, strengthen the body. Schoolgirls mostly pay attention to knowledge and seldom take care of their bodies. As a result, those who increase in knowledge and weaken in body. Girls who receive military training, activities, and exercises can strengthen their bodies.

Third, elucidate reason widely. In modern warfare, there are more and more sophisticated weapons. Artillery and smoke barriers are related to chemistry, and airplanes and submarines are related to physics. Lining up and shooting are related to mathematics. Receiving military training can also lead to academic research and benefit reason more clearly.

Fourth, maintain order. Soldiers practice, line up neatly, and their steps are aligned. They advance like wind and rain, retreat like mountains, stop like cutting feet, and walk like flowing water. The movement and stopping should be regular, and the advance and retreat should be moderate. Receiving military training can also cultivate strict discipline and a habit of maintaining order.

Fifth, respect obedience. In order to save the country from national crisis, it is valuable to unite the people of the whole country. The key to unity is to respect obedience. Only public freedom and public welfare, without private freedom and private welfare, and everyone is willing to obey the public opinion can avoid disturbances. Military training values obedience most. Women with this good habit are never a blessing for the future of the country.

The above is about the military training for girls in peacetime. If we talk about wartime, women who have received military training have more real power to serve the country. Everyone says that in wartime, women can engage in rescue work, guard in the rear, and be police in the inland. I think that even for the so-called rescue, guarding, and police work, it is not easy to try. They must have received military training and be proficient in national affairs to be competent. We women are not willing to talk emptily about saving the country, but we are willing to be practical. The national situation is extremely dangerous. If we do not prepare earnestly, we will perish ourselves. Everyone must not forget the war, and not care about death in war, in order to turn danger into safety and turn defeat into victory. My female compatriots, why don't you rise up together and receive military training to serve the country with your body? The future of the nation may be achievable.

Important News

Social Education Institutions in Jiangsu Province 109

Proposed Relief Measures for Provincial Education Funds (2)

It is imperative to request the Central Government to consider the extraordinary severity of the Jiangsu flood and to approve a reduction in revenue collection, while providing a monthly subsidy of 150,000 yuan to Jiangsu's education funds within the fiscal year of 1931 to maintain operations. In previous years, the Central Government had agreements for monthly subsidies to provinces with revenue deficits, such as Hubei and Anhui. Recently, due to the severe disaster in Hubei, the Central Government has reportedly increased the monthly subsidy to Hubei Province by 200,000 yuan, thereby sustaining its education funds. The extent and severity of the flood in Jiangsu this year are no less than those in Hubei. Just as the Central Government considered Hubei's situation previously, it should also consider Jiangsu's. Therefore, it is requested that the Central Government subsidize Jiangsu's education funds with 150,000 yuan monthly throughout the fiscal year of 1931 to ensure its sustenance. Since both Jiangsu and Hubei are disaster-stricken provinces facing similar difficulties, it is believed that the Central Government will treat them equally and provide assistance accordingly.

It is imperative to comply with the National Government's publicly announced "Trial Budget Regulations for the 1930 Fiscal Year of the Republic of China" and the "Standards for Dividing National and Local Revenues and Expenditures." The entire funding of the National Central University, amounting to 1,320,000 yuan, should be transferred to the Ministry of Finance for payment and no longer be managed by the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office. In August of the 18th year (1929), the 34th Political Affairs Conference resolved that the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office would permanently allocate 1,320,000 yuan annually to the National Central University. The reason for the term "permanently" at that time was that Jiangsu Province's special education funds included land tax levies and slaughter tax, which were national revenues. Therefore, it was acceptable for the Central University's funding to be permanently allocated by the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office annually. However, since the "Trial Budget Regulations for the 1930 Fiscal Year" were promulgated and implemented by the government, all land taxes and slaughter taxes have been designated as local revenues. Furthermore, the expenditure standards explicitly stipulate that the funding for national schools should be paid by the national government, not by local governments. Thus, the basis for the term "permanently" no longer exists in terms of revenue realities. More importantly, in terms of explicit legal provisions, since national and local revenues and expenditures have been divided, and major taxes like salt tax, cigarette tax, transit tax, and special tax have been designated as national revenues with the hope of increases, while fixed taxes like land tax, slaughter tax, and business tax have been designated as local revenues, the entire funding of 1,320,000 yuan for the Central University should be paid by the Ministry of Finance and no longer by the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office. This is not only just and reasonable but also a proper approach that is mutually beneficial rather than mutually destructive. Previously, the authorities of the Central University hoped that a portion of the university's funding would be permanently allocated by the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office because Jiangsu Province had special education funds that were considered more reliable. However, experience in recent years has shown that Jiangsu Province's special education funds not only suffer from annual revenue shortfalls of several hundred thousand yuan during normal times, but also the shortfalls increase significantly during famine years, with the total shortfall exceeding three million yuan in recent years. Previously, before the promulgation and implementation of the "Trial Budget Regulations for the 1930 Fiscal Year," the shortfall in funding revenue could be compensated by dreaming of additional education funds from the salt tax surcharge. Now, such dreams are absolutely prohibited, meaning there is no way to increase revenue. The authorities of the Central University and those who care about the Central University may still believe that although Jiangsu Province's special education funds suffer from annual shortfalls and lack avenues for increasing revenue, they still generate some revenue each year. Confucius said, "I am not concerned about scarcity but about inequality." Although the funds are not much, if they are distributed equally, they are still reliable. Furthermore, the Central University can receive at least 600,000 yuan annually from the Ministry of Finance in addition to the 1,320,000 yuan allocated by the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office. This dual approach seems very advantageous. However, the policy of equalizing scarcity and poverty will inevitably lead to mutual destruction. Moreover, at a time when Jiangsu Province's special education funds are facing extreme difficulties, while seeking funds from the Ministry of Finance, they still insist on obtaining funds from the Jiangsu Education Funds Management Office, making it even more difficult for provincial educational institutions that rely solely on the Management Office's funds without any support from the Ministry. How can they bear to do this? Therefore, for the sake of the Central University authorities and those who care about the Central University, it is imperative to follow the examples of several universities in Beiping and designate more reliable fixed funds for the Central University's funding, or follow the precedents of National Wuhan University and other universities and request approval to allocate the Central University's funding from the national taxes within Jiangsu and Anhui provinces, such as the salt tax. This approach would comply with the "Trial Budget Regulations for the 1930 Fiscal Year" and the "Standards for Dividing National and Local Revenues and Expenditures" promulgated by the National Government, alleviate the financial difficulties of Jiangsu Province's education funds, and prevent the Central University and Jiangsu's provincial educational institutions from suffering economic oppression or even perishing together. This is a superior strategy that is mutually beneficial rather than mutually destructive.

The above-mentioned remedial measures are based on facts and laws, which can somewhat alleviate the current financial difficulties of Jiangsu's education funds. It is respectfully requested that they be reviewed and implemented for the benefit of the public. (End)

Jiangsu Province 110

Petition from Representatives of the Provincial Elementary School Teachers' Association

The Education Department Accepts Suggestions, and the Provincial Party Headquarters Strongly Supports

The Executive Committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Elementary School Teachers' Association convened a meeting at the Zhenzhong Elementary School in Zhenjiang on the 24th of the month to vigorously advocate for the cessation of Central University's education funds. It was decided to appoint representatives from Zhenzhong Elementary School and Yangzhong Elementary School to petition the Education Department and the Provincial Party Headquarters. The representatives presented the petition and explained their intentions. Jiang and Deng accepted the representatives' suggestions and agreed to forward them to the department head. After accepting the representatives' suggestions, Ma stated that the Provincial Party Headquarters had already resolved to strive for the cessation of Central University's education funds during the provincial representative conference in August of this year and had jointly submitted a petition to the Central Government with the Provincial Government. Vocational Education Society Holds Oath Ceremony to Boycott Japanese Goods 113

At 8:00 AM yesterday, the staff of the Chinese Vocational Education Society's office and affiliated cooperative agencies, along with members of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Institute who have introduced achievements, members of the Work-Study Mutual Aid Society, and new family members, held a large-scale oath ceremony to boycott Japanese goods at the Chinese Vocational School. More than 2,000 people attended. The ceremony began with Chairman Jiang Wenyu reporting the significance of the oath and the attention paid by various parties to the society's actions. He emphasized that everyone should engrave the oath in their hearts, never forget it, resolutely implement it, and thoroughly sever economic ties with Japan. Next, attendees raised their right hands and recited the oath in unison: "I will never buy Japanese goods; my family will never buy Japanese goods; I will persuade my relatives and friends not to buy Japanese goods." The sound reverberated through the sky. Supervisor Zhu Ziqiao then delivered a speech, urging everyone to fulfill their oaths, persevere, and achieve tangible results after the ceremony. Han Zeidang, Mo Youcha, Huang Renzhi, and Pan Yangyi spoke successively. Huang Renzhi encouraged the audience to start with themselves when doing good deeds and reforming themselves when doing bad deeds, which deeply moved everyone. The passionate and inspiring oath ceremony concluded at around 10:00 AM. It is reported that the Chinese Vocational School Alumni Association also convened all alumni in Shanghai yesterday to participate in the oath and decided to re-elect the executive committee on New Year's Day. The Student Unrest at the Sino-French School Has Temporarily Ended 114

Most Students Scheduled to Return to Classes Today

The student unrest at the Sino-French School, established by the French in Shanghai, was triggered by the school's attempts to prevent students from organizing anti-Japanese associations and engaging in anti-Japanese activities. As for the remaining students who cannot return to school, the Sino-French School Anti-Japanese Association has arranged for them to be placed in other schools.

Students Returning from Japan 118

Shanghai Branch of the Anti-Japanese Association Membership Meeting

Adopts Constitution and Re-Elects Directors Using Postal Voting

Publishes Letter to Representatives of the Peace Conference and Letter to National Compatriots

The Shanghai Branch of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association of Students Returning from Japan held its first membership meeting at the Chinese Vocational Education Society on Hualong Road at 2:00 PM yesterday. More than 60 members, including Yang Zhengzi, attended. Ms. He Xuekuan, the association's executive director, chaired the meeting, and Wu Huiqing served as the recorder. After the ceremony, the chairman reported on the association's work since its establishment. Then, the meeting began to discuss and resolve six proposals: (1) Adopting the constitution: Resolved to adopt; (2) How to promote the development of the association: Resolved to publish more publications and focus on factual aspects; (3) Stipulating the association's financial issues: Resolved that the next executive committee will handle it according to the constitution; (4) Re-electing staff: Resolved that due to the insufficient number of attendees, postal voting will be used for the sake of caution, and the temporary executive committee will be responsible for completing it within one week; (5) The association should express its advice to the representatives of the peace conference: Resolved to publish; (6) Letter to national compatriots already drafted, please approve: Resolved to approve. The meeting adjourned.

The Patriotic United Association of Educational Circles in Shanghai is working extremely hard on anti-Japanese national salvation. Beijing-Guangdong 125

Representatives Take a Break Yesterday

Six Representatives from Guangdong Jointly Issue a Statement

The Beijing-Guangdong Peace and Unification Conference took a break yesterday and today, so there has been no progress in the discussions on party affairs. However, after the Beijing representatives Zhang Ji, Wu Tiecheng, and Chen Mingshu went to Beijing, they have been consulting on the three provisional measures for the Fourth Plenary Session that were determined the day before yesterday. It is expected that one of these three measures will be selected and implemented. It is also heard that implementing the first measure is more likely. Currently, Beijing representative Chen Mingshu and others have been approved to leave Beijing by overnight train tonight and are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai tomorrow. Immediately after arriving in Shanghai, they will hold the sixth preparatory meeting to decide on this issue. The details are recorded separately below:

The issue of the Fourth Plenary Congress: 126

Regarding the issue of party affairs, the Beijing and Guangdong representatives held an informal discussion focusing on the Fourth National Congress as the core when they held a talk the day before yesterday. Other issues regarding party affairs have not yet been discussed. According to a person speaking on behalf of the Beijing representatives, one of the three provisional measures for convening the meeting will be selected and implemented. It is expected that the first measure is the closest to both sides, and the difficulties are fewer (i.e., convening the meeting on schedule, etc.). However, it cannot be considered completely certain at present. It will have to wait until the Beijing and Guangdong representatives hold the sixth preparatory meeting tomorrow morning to decide.

A meeting was held at the Hu residence yesterday morning: 127

At 10:00 AM yesterday, the Guangdong representatives Wang Jingwei, Sun Ke, Li Wenfan, Chen Youren, Wu Chaochu, and others went to the Hu residence to hold a discussion. Zou Haibin also participated despite his illness. The six Guangdong representatives discussed the future of the peace conference for a long time, dispersing at 12:00 PM. The contents of the discussion were not disclosed because they were an exchange of views among the Guangdong delegation members. However, the contents discussed were still related to the issue of party reform.

Guangdong Representatives' Interview: 128

Yesterday, reporters interviewed the Guangdong representatives Wang, Sun, Wu, Zou, Li, and Chen. The gentlemen jointly issued the following statement: (Question) If Mr. Chiang Kai-shek fulfills his previous statement and resolutely steps down, has the Guangdong side considered his future position? (Answer) Before departing from Guangzhou, the colleagues repeatedly discussed Mr. Chiang's appointment to the Northern Expedition in the fifteenth year, and his achievements are recognized by the people of the country (omitted). Therefore, if Mr. Chiang can fulfill his previous statement this time and resign from the position of Chairman of the National Government, the colleagues in Guangdong intend to propose that Mr. Chiang serve as Chairman of the National Defense Committee. Firstly, national defense is important in the face of national crisis, and secondly, his talents will not be wasted. If the central political system reform plan can be passed and implemented this time, the Chairman of the National Government will not bear actual administrative responsibility and should be held by someone who is old, virtuous, and can serve as a national model. Mr. Chiang has always taken it upon himself to work hard for the national revolution, so it is more appropriate for him to serve as Chairman of the National Defense Committee than as Chairman of the National Government.

Wang Jingwei will move: 129

Wang Jingwei currently resides in Sir Robert Ho Tung's residence on Gordon Road. The visits from various circles every day are limited, which Wang finds inconvenient. Therefore, he has rented a new residence at No. 774 Xinpushi Road, which is currently being renovated. He will move in as soon as the work is completed.

Zhao Pilian's interview: 130

Zhao Pilian and Jia Jingde, important figures in Shanxi Province, came to Shanghai the day before yesterday to represent Shanxi in the peace conference and have already met with Guangdong representative Wang Jingwei and others. The reporter from Huadong News Agency interviewed him at his residence yesterday. According to Zhao, this trip south is not a so-called mission. He only hopes that in the face of foreign aggression, the country will unite as one to seek the realization of great unity in order to secure domestic stability and resist foreign aggression. The rumors that Mr. Yan Xishan and Feng Yuxiang will go south are not true. The purpose of my trip is to actively hope for sincere cooperation between Nanjing and Guangdong. In addition, I intend to represent Yan Xishan and attend the peace conference when it is officially held.

Li Shizeng enters the hospital: 131

Beijing representative Li Shizeng only attended the peace preparatory meeting once and then entered the Zhongben Sanatorium for treatment due to a minor illness. According to Zeng Zhongming, Wang Jingwei's secretary, yesterday, Li is suffering from a throat ailment, and his condition has slightly improved since entering the hospital for treatment.

Zou Lu met guests yesterday: 132

Zou Lu has not participated in the meetings for days due to illness, and he does not always go to the Hu residence. After being treated by traditional Chinese medicine doctor Chuan Zhongren, his illness has greatly improved. He can eat normally and met with Zhang Fakui, Ke Xing'e, Yi Peiji, and many others yesterday.

Wei Daofeng visited Wang yesterday: 133

Wei Daofeng, a representative from the Northeast, visited Wang Jingwei yesterday at 4:00 PM, but Wang was out.

The Anti-Japanese Association Uncovers 134

Zheng Zenan's Bribery to Release Goods

Zheng is the Chairman of the Sugar Industry Association

Releasing White Sugar after Receiving a Bribe of 3,000 Yuan

Also Bribed the Anti-Japanese Association with 1,000 Yuan

The Anti-Japanese Association held its 15th executive meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday. Executive Committee members Wang Xiaolai, Lin Lianhou, Wang Yansong, Lu Jingshi, Chen Tingrui, Fang Jiaobo, and others attended. In addition to discussing various important cases, the Tax Bureau reported the bribery case of Zheng Zenan, Chairman of the Refined Sugar Association. The Executive Committee believed that the case was serious and must be thoroughly investigated. It was decided that the informant, Zhu Anqing, should be released immediately, and the official, Ju Jiqiu, who refused the bribe should be rewarded. The following is a record of the reports:

Secretariat Submits Report to the Standing Committee Concerning the Bribery Case Involving the Sugar Industry Association 135

Regarding the matter of seeking review and approval for the report on the Sugar Industry Association's bribery scheme: On October 27th, Zhu Anqing secretly reported that Zheng Zenan, Chairman of the Sugar Industry Association, had extorted 3,000 yuan from sugar firms such as Yuan Damao He. We immediately dispatched Ju Jiqiu to secretly investigate. Now, according to the investigation report, Yuan Da firm did indeed pay 1,500 yuan as a national salvation fund on October 20th (Jiufeng Zhuang check). Mao He firm recorded 1,500 yuan as a temporary item under their name. Both firms' ledgers and a donation receipt from the Sugar Industry Elementary School were brought back. We immediately endorsed on the original report: (Ledgers etc. are temporarily stored, and any other information should be promptly investigated and reported.) While verifying, Ju Jiqiu reported that on October 31st at 1 PM, Zhu Anfu (owner of Shengji Sugar Firm and former executive committee member of the Sugar Industry Association) invited him to the Jue Lu Hotel, Room 76, for a secret meeting. He said that Chairman Zheng Zenan urgently wanted to settle the matter and offered 1,000 yuan to perfunctorily resolve it, including the original bribe of 1,000 yuan and a notice from the Jue Lu Hotel, which were submitted. This morning, around 11 AM, the original informant, Zhu Anqing (reportedly Zhu Anfu's younger brother), came to confess that Anqing had secretly reported the Sugar Industry Association's extortion from Yuan Yu and Mao He sugar firms. Now, because the committee members of the Sugar Industry Association feared a leak, they privately entrusted his elder brother, Zhu Anfu, to persuade you with 1,000 yuan to settle the matter. Today, he was asked to come to your office to retrieve the ledgers, assuring that the matter would absolutely not be publicized (a written confession is attached as evidence). Considering his contradictory behavior, he was detained. All the circumstances of the Sugar Industry Association's extortion and bribery are hereby reported to your committee for review and severe punishment to deter wickedness. Ju Jiqiu's resourcefulness in handling the matter should be rewarded. Respectfully submitted to the Standing Committee, with two reports from Ju Jiqiu, 1,000 yuan in bribes (banknotes), Zhu Anqing's interview notice, a letter of proof from Yuan Yu Firm, two ledgers, one receipt, Zhu Anqing's confession record, and one Jue Lu Hotel notice.

Ju Jiqiu's First Report 136

Regarding the report:

I was ordered to investigate the case of Yuan Yu, Mao He, and other sugar firms on Xian Gua Street and Yong An Street being extorted 3,000 yuan by Zheng Zenan, Chairman of the Sugar Industry Association. I went to Yuan Yu Firm on Xian Gua Street to inquire about everything and carefully reviewed the ledgers. I saw that on October 20th, 1,500 yuan had been paid to the National Salvation Fund, check number Jiufeng Zhuang. I immediately ordered them to produce the receipt for the National Salvation Fund. The firm took out a receipt issued by Zheng Zenan, which stated "Donation to the Sugar Industry Private Elementary School." The fact that the National Salvation Fund was transformed into a donation was suspicious. I took one ledger and one receipt, issuing a receipt, and went to Mao He Firm on Shui An Street. I also first requested the ledgers for review and saw that 1,500 yuan had been paid under the name "Temporary Record." This unusual item seemed suspicious, and the amount matched the 3,000 yuan mentioned in the secret report. Considering the seriousness of this matter, I did not dare to make a decision on my own and brought the ledger back for verification. After further investigation, I learned that the two firms intended to transport a large batch of Japanese goods to other ports. The matter was discovered at the docks, and it was reported to Chairman Zheng Zenan. Zheng said that if 3,000 yuan could be used as a national salvation fund, the goods could be released. The two firms immediately agreed to this. Whether this is true or not requires further investigation. The circumstances of the investigation are hereby reported for your review.

Ju Jiqiu's Second Report 137

Regarding the continuation of the report:

Since I was ordered to investigate the case of Sugar Industry Chairman Zheng Zenan's bribery of 3,000 yuan, someone persuaded me to accept a bribe of 1,000 yuan to avoid reporting the matter. Because the inside story was not clear, I pretended to agree. On October 31st, someone brought a note asking me to go to the Jue Lu Hotel for negotiations. I consulted Secretary Yan, who allowed me to go. At 2 PM, I went to Room 76 on the second floor of Jue Lu Hotel and met the contact person, Zhu Anfu. I learned that Mr. Zhu is the owner of Shengji Sugar Firm, located on Yanghang Street, and a former executive committee member of the Sugar Industry Association. During the meeting, Zhu Anfu said that Chairman Zheng (Zenan) urgently wanted to settle the matter and offered 1,000 yuan as compensation, asking me to perfunctorily investigate and maintain both parties' reputation. He immediately handed over 1,000 yuan in cash and repeatedly pleaded. I immediately stated that I didn't know if Mr. Zheng knew about or agreed to this money. Zhu Anfu said that he was ordered by Mr. Zheng to handle the matter and that Mr. Zheng also wished to resolve the matter. I made an excuse to go to the office to retrieve the ledgers. Zhu Anfu was very happy. I returned to the office and temporarily stored the 1,000 yuan with the accounting section of the Secretariat. The circumstances of the negotiations are hereby reported for your review.

Confession of the original informant, Zhu Anqing:

Anqing secretly reported that the Sugar Industry Association extorted bribes from Yuan Yu and Mao He sugar firms. Now, because the committee members of the Sugar Industry Association feared a leak, they privately entrusted his elder brother, Zhu Anfu, to persuade you with 1,000 yuan to settle the matter. Today, he was asked to come to your office to retrieve the ledgers, assuring that the matter would absolutely not be publicized. Zhu Anqing, November 1st.

Commander of the U.S. Far East Army 138

Major General Haines Arrives in Shanghai

To Return to the Philippines Tomorrow Morning

The Da Mei Evening News reports that Major General Haines, Commander of the U.S. Far East Army, arrived in Shanghai on Saturday night from Beijing and is staying at the Cathay Hotel. His wife and son accompanied him. Yesterday, U.S. Consul General Cunningham visited him. This morning (2nd), U.S. Minister Johnson also visited him at the Cathay Hotel. When reporters asked about the Philippine political situation, General Haines declined to comment. It is reported that Haines is stationed in the Philippines and commands the Far East Army, with a total of 10,500 U.S. Army personnel stationed in the Philippines. There are also 900 personnel stationed in Tianjin. As far as he knows, the number of troops stationed at this time should not increase or decrease. This time, he first inspected the U.S. troops in Tianjin, then took a train south, stayed in Nanjing for a few hours, and then came to Shanghai. He is scheduled to return to the Philippines by the Taifu Tuo Lun on Wednesday morning.

Whereabouts of Prominent Figures 139

Cai Yuanpei, Wang Boqun, Zheng Hongnian, and Japanese Consul Uemura took the night train to Beijing yesterday.

Chen Mingshu took the night train from Beijing yesterday and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

Dr. Eddy to Arrive in Shanghai 140

When the Shenyang Incident occurred, Dr. Eddy happened to be in the area conducting a large-scale evangelistic campaign. Dr. Eddy witnessed the various conspiracies and atrocities of the Japanese army's unwarranted occupation of Shenyang. He telegraphed the League of Nations in Geneva, the U.S. Secretary of State, and the British Foreign Minister, detailing the Japanese army's violent occupation of various parts of the Eastern Provinces, violating principles of justice and humanity, and their plan to permanently occupy Manchuria. He requested advocacy for justice and the maintenance of world peace. After that, Dr. Eddy traveled to Harbin, Tianjin, Beiping, Taiyuan, Jinan, and other places to lecture on the Japanese army's armed occupation of Shenyang on the evening of September 18th and the lawless actions in various parts of the Eastern Provinces in the following days. At the same time, he also gave systematic lectures on international politics, economics, society, and religion, which were well received by people in various places. However, in Beiping, he was strongly opposed by the Beiping communists. Dr. Eddy, at the invitation of the National Association of YMCAs, has set out for Shanghai and will arrive on the 4th of this month. It is reported that Dr. Eddy will stay in Shanghai for a day or two and then travel south to give public lectures to people in this city, which will be scheduled for early December. Dr. Eddy has written books such as "The Truth About Soviet Russia," "Sex and Youth," "Religion and Social Justice," "Eight Great Men," and "Faith in the New Era," all of which have been translated and published by the YMCA Publishing House.

A Record of the Return of Merchants from Japan 141

Japanese Force Merchants to Fix Silver

The Japanese firms in the Xingsheng Street area of the French Concession, such as Dachengxiang, have the largest operations. In light of the rampant violence of the Japanese, they would rather sacrifice economic ties with Japan and switch to operating domestic goods. They telegraphed their resident merchant Zhu Wende in Japan to wind up operations and return home. It turned out that there were already fixed but undelivered goods worth about 100,000 taels of silver. The Japanese refused to refund the deposit and would not allow him to return home until the silver was cleared. After Zhu telegraphed urging the money, the firms, having traded with Japan for decades, could not bear such extortion and reluctantly remitted the silver in full. Therefore, Zhu Wende returned home yesterday.

National Government Purchases 142

U.S. Wheat Begins to Arrive in Shanghai Today

First Ship Enters Port Today, Docking at North Bund

127,000 Tons in Three Months

American Business Fu Lai Shipping Undertakes Transport

The U.S. wheat relief to China has been previously reported in detail in this newspaper. The British Tianxiang Shipping only undertook one shipment, which did not arrive due to sea conditions. The shipments that have already arrived in Shanghai are orders from the three new factories in this city. Now, this relief wheat has been shipped by a large number of commercial vessels dispatched by the American Fu Lai Shipping. The details of this matter are recorded as follows:

The American Company Wins the Bid for China’s Order of a Large Amount of American Relief Wheat, Totaling 450,000 Tons. The Shipping Method Is to Ship in Batches to China. This Year, Over 100,000 Tons Will Be Shipped First, and the Remaining Will Continue to Be Shipped Next Spring. Because the Water Feet Must Be Short and Cheap, Bids Were Held in Shanghai. At that time, the Local Shipping Companies All Went to Bid at the Lowest Price. At that time, the British Shipping Companies All Bid at US$3.10 per Ton, and the American Fu Lai Bid at US$2.90 per Ton. At the Time of Bidding, It Was Won by the American Fu Lai. Therefore, This Large Consignment of Relief Wheat Was Shipped by American Ships.

Tianxiang First Shipped When the British Tianxiang Shipping Was Also One of the Bidders. The Water Feet It Recognized Was the Second Shortest Price, But the First Batch of Relief Wheat Was Shipped From the United States. The Shanghai Shipping Tender Was Not Yet Public, So It Was First Entrusted to the British Tianxiang Shipping to Send a Norwegian Ship Named Nuolja, From Portland, USA, to Ship 7,260 Tons to Shanghai, Starting on October 6. This Is the First Batch of American Relief Wheat to China, Which Will Enter Port Today.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce 143

Advises to Avoid Japanese Ships

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday replied to the China Chemical Industry Society, stating: "We acknowledge receipt of your letter of the 31st of this month, stating that you have ordered butter from Australia and that the goods have been shipped to Yokohama. If these goods are transshipped onto Japanese ships, misunderstandings may arise. We hereby state the following processing situation for your reference: (1) The Anti-Japanese Association's fifth executive committee meeting has already resolved the matter of refusing to load foreign goods onto Japanese ships. Your company should send a telegram stating that you should avoid Japanese ships when transshipping. In short, your company should make every effort to do so within the realm of possibility. This chamber will still forward the situation described in your letter to the Anti-Japanese Association. (2) When ordering goods from Europe and the United States in the future, you must first declare that they must not be loaded onto Japanese ships, otherwise the goods will be returned and all losses will be compensated. This should be agreed upon in advance to avoid temporary disputes."

Preparations for the National Striving Association 144

A Discussion Meeting Was Held Yesterday at the YMCA

Huang Jingwan, Wu Mai, Zhu Lin, Miao Zhijie, Zhou Wenji, and others, in light of the Japanese relentless invasion of China, organized the China Self-Strengthening Society to act as the government's support. The society held a discussion meeting yesterday at the YMCA and renamed itself the National Striving Association. Its purpose is to continuously strive with a fearless spirit, so that everyone has the determination to love the country. Zhou Wenji was recommended to draft the articles, which will be formally established in the near future.

Victims of the Shenyang Ordnance Factory 145

Petitioned in Beijing Yesterday

Demanding that the Ministry of Military Affairs Find a Way to Resettle Them

The victims of the Shenyang Ordnance Factory, who escaped danger and arrived in Shanghai, organized a petition and maintenance group to request the municipal government to find a way to maintain their current livelihoods and resettle their work. Although the municipal government has telegraphed the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ordnance Department to set up Jiang An to resettle them, there has been no response. The first two batches have been issued relief funds of four yuan each by the National Government Relief Committee, but the meager relief funds are of no use and have long been exhausted. After exhausting all avenues, the congress resolved that the first batch should appoint Yu Lin Gui and Li Chanxi as representatives to take the 11:45 PM Beijing-Shanghai night train to Beijing yesterday to petition, demanding that the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Ordnance Department find a way to resettle them. The third batch has also appointed Lin Mei and Liu Shaomei to take the night express train to Beijing today to continue the petition.

Municipal Government Orders 146

Expediting Coordination of Labor-Management Disputes

Page 10

Strictly Preventing Strikes and Work Stoppages

After the violent Japanese occupation of our Liaoning, the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department issued a notice to all trade associations and labor unions, limiting them to resolve all labor-management disputes within two weeks. The municipal government yesterday received a telegram from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating that at this time of national crisis, all Chinese people should work together to await government measures. Workers in various places should work hard to produce and overcome difficulties together. Labor-management disputes should be resolved immediately, and attention should be paid to preventing strikes and work stoppages. It is hoped that the relevant government agencies in various places will follow this directive and transfer it to all labor and management organizations. The Municipal Government yesterday instructed the competent authorities of this Municipality, the Bureau of Social Affairs, to transfer and order the labor and management organizations to follow the instructions.

Chinese Seamen's Union Sealed Yesterday 147

Since the establishment of the Organizing Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union on July 21st this year, under the orders of the Central Committee, three months have passed. Unexpectedly, at noon yesterday, several bailiffs from the Shanghai Local Court, together with the police in charge, went to seal the premises on the grounds that the former Chinese Seamen's Industrial Union owed rent. The union staff declared to them that this was the Organizing Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union, a legal institution directly under the Central Party Headquarters, and had no connection with the former Industrial Union. However, the bailiffs ignored the facts and claimed that they were acting under the orders of the Local Court to seal the premises. It is reported that the union has reported the situation to the Central Committee and requested a thorough investigation and strict questioning of the Shanghai Local Court.

Merchants Need Not Organize Merchant Corps 148

Reply Telegram from the Ministry of Military Affairs

The National Chamber of Commerce Federation previously decided at a provisional supervisory committee meeting to request the government to restore the training of merchants in military knowledge, so that they could serve as a backup for the government in the event of war with foreign countries. After this request, the Ministry of Military Affairs sent a telegram to the Shanghai National Chamber of Commerce Federation yesterday, stating: "We have received your telegram of the day before yesterday requesting the establishment of merchant corps, which has been forwarded to the Ministries of Interior and Industry for verification. According to their replies, merchants need not organize merchant corps, and the Legislative Yuan has reviewed and approved the National Government's record. We hereby inform you of this fact." Ministry of Military Affairs, Urgent.

Another New Naval Aircraft 149

Scheduled for Test Flight on the 12th

The two aircraft manufactured by the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office were completed the day before yesterday. The Jianghe was tested on the Longhua River surface with good results. Now the Jiangfeng, named by the Naval Department, has also been completed. All internal structures, components, and other aspects are not much different from the Jianghe. The new aircraft has also been scheduled to fly over the Longhua River surface at 9 AM on the 12th of this month.

Foreign Warship Movements 150

U.S. Warships to the Philippines: The U.S. Destroyer Squadron stationed in China was transferred from Yantai to Shanghai on the 19th of last month, totaling fourteen ships. Later, three ships sailed first, and the remaining eleven ships have now been ordered to sail from Shanghai to Manila with the cruiser Black Hawk leading the destroyers including 212 and Gumnson.

Japanese Warship Deployments: The Yangtze River stationed ships belonging to the First Foreign Dispatch Team of Japan have been reorganized by the Japanese naval commander in Shanghai since November 1. Four ships are stationed in Shanghai, five in Hankou, three in Yichang, and one each in Changsha and Shashi. There are two ships each in Nanjing and Jiujiang, and one each in Wuhu and Daye. In the South China region, there is one ship each in Guangdong and Fujian, and two in Shantou. In the North China region, there is one ship each in Yantai, Longkou, Lushun, and Qingdao, and one in Xiamen, totaling thirty ships.
